    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split(' ')
    date[0] = date[0][:2]
    date[1] = date[1][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:4]
    date[3] = date[3][:4]
    date[4] = date[4][:4]
    date[5] = date[5][:4]
    date[6] = date[6][:4]
    date[7] = date[7][:4]
    date[8] = date[8][:4]
    date[9] = date[9][:4]
    date[10] = date[10][:4]
    date[11] = date[11][:4]
    date[12] = date[12][:4]
    date[13]

    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split(' ')
    date[0] = date[0][:2]
    date[1] = date[1][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:4]
    date[3] = date[3][:4]
    date[4] = date[4][:4]
    date[5] = date[5][:4]
    date[6] = date[6][:4]
    date[7] = date[7][:4]
    date[8] = date[8][:4]
    date[9] = date[9][:4]
    date[10] = date[10][:4]
    date[11] = date[11][:4]
    date[12] = date[12][:4]
    date[13] = date[13][:4]
    date[14] = date[14][:4]
    date[15] = date[15][:4]
    date[16] = date[16][:4]
    date[17] = date[17][

    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split(' ')
    date[0] = date[0][:2]

'''Write a function to convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
def ical_to_date(date):
    '''Convert a date of yyyy-mm-dd format to dd-mm-yyyy format.'''
    date = date.split(' ')
    date[0] = date[0][:2]
    date[1] = date[1][:2]
    date[2] = date[2][:4]
    date[3] = date[3][:4]
